Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices— 1991 


RELEASED:   MAY  1992 

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  estimates 
for  Montana.   These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey 
conducted  in  the  fall  of  1991.    Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and 
ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  1991  acreage  and 
production  of  different  crops.   About  5,000  questionnaires  were  tabulated.   Thanks  to 
those  who  participated!

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county 
estimates  for  Montana.   These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production 
survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  1992.   Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  fanners 
and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  1992  acreage  and 
production  of  different  crops.   About  5,300  questionnaires  were  tabulated.   Thanks  to 
those  who  participated!

Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices— 1993 


RELEASED:  March  1994 

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county 
estimates  for  Montana.   These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production 
survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  1993.    Questionnaires  v^ere  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers 
and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  1993  acreage  and 
production  of  different  crops.   About  5,300  questionnaires  were  tabulated.   Thanks  to 
those  w^ho  participated! 


James  K.  Sands 
State  Statistician

MONTANA  STATE  LIBRARY 

RELEASED:   March  1995  helena'm^ontan''aI9620 


The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates 
for  Montana.    These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey 
conducted  in  the  fall  of  1994.   Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers 
throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  1994  acreage  and  production  of  different 
crops.    About  9,000  questionnaires  were  tabulated.   Thanks  to  those  who  participated! 


James  K.  Sands 
State  Statistician

Serving  Montana  Agriculture

Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices— 1995 


RELEASED:   March  1996 


The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates 
for  Montana.  These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted 
in  the  fall  of  1995.   Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout 
Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  1995  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.   About 
8,000  questioimaires  were  tabulated.   Thanks  to  those  who  participated! 


"f— 


Peggy  Stringer 
State  Statistician

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana. 
These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  1996. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  fanners  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on 
the  1996  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  8,000  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to 
those  who  participated!

^  The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana. 

These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  1997. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on 
the  1997  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  8,000  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to 
those  who  participated!

Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices- 1999 


RELEASED:  February  18,  2000 


The  Montana  Agiicultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana. 
These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fail  of  1999. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the 
1999  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  7,500  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those 
who  participated!  Croppmg  practice  estimates  were  funded  by  the  Montana  Wheat  &  Barley  Committee. 


,^ 


Peggy  Stringer 

State  Statistician

The  Montana  Agncultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana, 
^rhese  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  2000. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the 
2000  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  7,500  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those 
who  participated!  Cropping  practice  estimates  were  funded  by  the  Montana  Wheat  &  Barley  Committee. 


Peggy  Stringer

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana. 
These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  2000. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the 
2000  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  7,500  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those 
who  participated!  Cropping  practice  estimates  were  funded  by  the  Montana  Wheat  &  Barley  Committee. 


Peggy  Stringer 
State  Statistician

Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices-2002 


RELEASED:  February  2 1,  2003 


The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana. 
These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  2002. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  fanners  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the 
2002  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  6,500  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those 
who  participated!

Peggy  Stringer

Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices-2003 


RELEASED:  February  12,  2004 

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Service  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estimates  for  Montana. 
These  county  statistics  are  based  on  an  acreage  and  production  survey  conducted  in  the  fall  of  2003. 
Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the 
2003  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  6,900  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those 
who  participated! 


^/- 


Peggy  Stnnger 
State  Statistician

The  Montana  Agricultural  Statistics  Sen/ice  compiles  the  only  annual  county  estinnates  for 
Montana.  These  county  statistics  are  based  on  acreage  and  production  surveys  conducted  during 
the  fall  of  2004.  Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers  throughout  Montana 
asking  for  information  on  the  2004  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops.  About  6,900 
questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those  who  participated!

United  States  Department  of  Agriculture  •  10  West  15'"  St.,  Suite  3100  Helena,  MT  59626

Montana  Barley  Estimates 

By  Counties  and  Cropping  Practices  -  2005 


Released:  February  17,  2006 

. .  ,  ISia  I.  fth  AVE. 
8QENA.  MCMTANA  59620 

USDA,  National  Agricultural  Statistics  Service,  Montana  Field  Office  compiles  the  only  annual 
county  estimates  for  Montana.  These  county  statistics  are  based  on  acreage  and  production  surveys 
conducted  during  the  fall  of  2005.  Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers 
throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  2005  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops. 
About  8,200  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those  who  participated! 


7^/  ^.h 

Peggy  Stringer

Released:  February  13,  2007 


o; 


USDA,  National  Agricultural  Statistics  Service,  Montana  Field  Office  compiles  the  only  annual 
county  estimates  for  Montana.  These  county  statistics  are  based  on  acreage  and  production  surveys 
conducted  during  the  fall  of  2006.  Questionnaires  were  sent  to  a  sample  of  farmers  and  ranchers 
throughout  Montana  asking  for  information  on  the  2006  acreage  and  production  of  different  crops. 
About  5,846  questionnaires  were  tabulated.  Thanks  to  those  who  participated!
